Use the !sr command to request songs in the format of:
!sr game - title
The bot searches for the closest match to "game" and "song", example:
!sr Wind Waker - treta discovered

Requests display on stream, the first Image "0" is the currently playing song. The following three "1", "2", "3" are in queue for you to vote to play next.
If you're on desktop you can click on the icons to vote. If you're on mobile you can vote using !vote 1 , !vote 2 , !vote 3
